# Issue 21072: Beta-adic tools

archive/issues_020835.json:
```json
{
    "body": "This is a big set of tools to manipulate beta-expansions described by automata.\nAutomata are completely re-implemented in C language and with very efficient functions.\nIt is the continuation of #16723 with adaptations to make it work on linux and with sage 7.2.\nNow it is merged with sage 8.6.rc1\n\n\nCC:  @slel dbenielli mercatp\n\nKeywords: beta-adic, automata, regular languages\n\nAuthor: Paul Mercat\n\nBranch: public/b-adic\n\nStatus: new\n\nCommit: 064ca911adc256ecd093004da65f2bf29f526975\n\nIssue created by migration from https://trac.sagemath.org/ticket/21072\n\n",
```

This is a big set of tools to manipulate beta-expansions described by automata.
Automata are completely re-implemented in C language and with very efficient functions.
It is the continuation of #16723 with adaptations to make it work on linux and with sage 7.2.
Now it is merged with sage 8.6.rc1


CC:  @slel dbenielli mercatp

Keywords: beta-adic, automata, regular languages

Author: Paul Mercat

Branch: public/b-adic

Status: new

Commit: 064ca911adc256ecd093004da65f2bf29f526975

Issue created by migration from https://trac.sagemath.org/ticket/21072

``````diff
 Automata are completely re-implemented in C language and with very efficient functions.
 It is the continuation of #16723 with adaptations to make it work on linux and with sage 7.2.
``````

``````diff
+Now it is merged with sage 8.1.
``````
